
###########################################
#
# Plot Events
#
# ID 7000-8299 is reserved
#
###########################################
# Blackmail									7250-7270
# Drunken Plot Member						7040-7045
#
# Ultimatum event series					8000-8099
# Plot to kill character 					8220-8227
#
# Assassination notification events			8250-8299
#											7700-7999


###########################################
# Blackmail
###########################################
# 7250-7270

# The plot has been leaked
character_event = {
	id = 7250
	desc = "EVTDESC7250"
	picture = GFX_evt_spymaster
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes

	trigger = {
		has_plot = yes
		is_plot_active = no
		num_of_plot_backers = 1
		any_courtier = {
			has_job_title = job_spymaster
			NOT = { is_plot_target_of = ROOT }
		}
		top_liege = {
			any_realm_lord = {
				OR = {
					higher_tier_than = BARON
					is_patrician = yes
				}
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_plot_target_of = ROOT }
				any_backed_character = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
				employer = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
				NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			any_plot_backer = {
				trait = imbecile
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			any_plot_backer = {
				trait = lunatic
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			num_of_plot_backers = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			num_of_plot_backers = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			num_of_plot_backers = 6
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			num_of_plot_backers = 8
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 15
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 20
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7250" #Can my spymaster never bring me good news?
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_realm_lord = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						higher_tier_than = BARON
						is_patrician = yes
					}
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_plot_target_of = ROOT }
					any_backed_character = {
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					employer = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
					NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 } }
				}
				letter_event = { id = 7255 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail or not
letter_event = {
	id = 7255
	desc = "EVTDESC7255"
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = { reveal_plot = ROOT }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7255" #A little blackmail can't hurt
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = {
					plot_target_char = {
						OR = {
							NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -25 } }
							is_rival = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = {
					plot_target_char = {
						OR = {
							has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
							is_allied_with = ROOT
							reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 50 }
							is_friend = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { letter_event = { id = 7260 days = 1 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7260" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7255" #Reveal it
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = diligent
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = {
					plot_target_char = {
						OR = {
							NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -25 } }
							is_rival = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					plot_target_char = {
						any_courtier = {
							has_job_title = job_spymaster
						}
					}
				}
				reveal_plot_w_message = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					plot_target_char = {
						NOT = {
							any_courtier = {
								has_job_title = job_spymaster
							}
						}
					}
				}
				reveal_plot = yes
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = devious_plotter
					who = PREV
					months = 120
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						liege = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
					}
					liege = {
						opinion = {
							who = PREVPREV
							modifier = devious_plotter
							months = 120
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7255" #It does not concern me
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = slothful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = content
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -50 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Bounce event (when blackmail done by diplo-action)
character_event = {
	id = 7259
	
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = { letter_event = { id = 7260 } }
	}
}

# Blackmail attempt
letter_event = {
	id = 7260
	desc = "EVTDESC7260"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7260" #Give in
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { wealth = 100 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				wealth = 250
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = paranoid
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = deceitful
			}
		}
		wealth = -100
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_blackmailed
			years = 10
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = { letter_event = { id = 7265 days = 3 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7260" #I won't tolerate blackmail!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_failed_blackmail
			multiplier = 2
			years = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					any_courtier = {
						has_job_title = job_spymaster
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot_w_message = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					NOT = {
						any_courtier = {
							has_job_title = job_spymaster
						}
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot = yes
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = devious_plotter
				who = ROOT
				months = 120
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					liege = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
				}
				liege = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = devious_plotter
						months = 120
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = { letter_event = { id = 7270 days = 3 } }
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail succeded
letter_event = {
	id = 7265
	desc = "EVTDESC7265"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EXCELLENT"
		treasury = 100
		clr_character_flag = attempted_blackmail
	}
}

###########################################
# Drunken Plot Member
###########################################
# 7040-7045

# Drunk plot member spills the beans - Non-Murder Plots
character_event = {
	id = 7040
	desc = "EVTDESC7040"
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {
		any_backed_character = {
			has_plot = yes
			NOR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}
			is_plot_active = no
			OR = {
				NOT = { religion_group = muslim }
				trait = hedonist
				trait = drunkard
			}
			NOR = {
				has_character_flag = event7041
				plot_target_char = {
					any_known_plotter = { character = PREVPREV }
				}
			}
		}
		NOR = {
			trait = temperate
			is_smart_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 300
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = drunkard
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = imbecile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			OR = {
				trait = slow
				trait = dull
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { intrigue = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 8
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 15
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 20
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7040"
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				has_plot = yes
				NOR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					has_plot = plot_take_revenge
				}
				is_plot_active = no
				NOR = {
					has_character_flag = event7041
					plot_target_char = {
						any_known_plotter = { character = PREVPREV }
					}
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = revealed_plot
				months = 120
			}
			set_character_flag = event7040
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = { id = 7045 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Plot revealed by drunken backer
character_event = {
	id = 7045
	desc = "EVTDESC7045"
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7045"
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					any_courtier = {
						has_job_title = job_spymaster
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot_w_message = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					NOT = {
						any_courtier = {
							has_job_title = job_spymaster
						}
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_plot = plot_seduce }
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = devious_plotter
					who = ROOT
					months = 120
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						independent = no
						liege = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
					}
					liege = {
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = devious_plotter
							months = 120
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Drunk plot member spills the beans - Murder Plots
character_event = {
	id = 7041
	desc = EVTDESC7040
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {
		any_backed_character = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}
			is_plot_active = no
			OR = {
				NOT = { religion_group = muslim }
				trait = hedonist
				trait = drunkard
			}
			NOR = {
				has_character_flag = event7041
				plot_target_char = {
					any_known_plotter = { character = PREVPREV }
				}
			}
		}
		NOR = {
			trait = temperate
			is_smart_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 600

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = drunkard
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = imbecile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			OR = {
				trait = slow
				trait = dull
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { intrigue = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 8
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 15
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			intrigue = 20
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7040
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					has_plot = plot_take_revenge
				}
				NOT = { has_character_flag = event7041 }
				NOT = {
					plot_target_char = {
						any_known_plotter = {	character = PREVPREV }
					}
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = revealed_plot
				months = 120
			}
			set_character_flag = event7041
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = { id = 7046 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Murder plot revealed by drunken backer
character_event = {
	id = 7046
	desc = EVTDESC7045
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7045
		
		clr_character_flag = event7041
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					any_courtier = {
						has_job_title = job_spymaster
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot_w_message = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					NOT = {
						any_courtier = {
							has_job_title = job_spymaster
						}
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot = yes
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = devious_plotter
				who = ROOT
				months = 120
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					independent = no
					liege = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
				}
				liege = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = devious_plotter
						months = 120
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				NOR = {
					trait = lunatic
					trait = possessed
					independent = yes
					has_plot = plot_take_revenge
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = abort_plot
		}
	}
}

###########################################
# Ultimatum event series
###########################################
# 8000-8120

# Ultimatum - Install Pretender
letter_event = {
	id = 8036
	desc = "EVTDESC8036"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = { leads_faction = faction_pretender }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			clr_character_flag = civil_war_faction_leader
			clr_character_flag = civil_war_faction_member
			clr_character_flag = will_join_civil_war
			diplomatic_immunity = yes 
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_pretender
				clr_character_flag = civil_war_faction_member
				clr_character_flag = will_join_civil_war
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				FROM = {
					supported_claimant_title = {
						is_primary_holder_title = no
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					supported_claimant_title = {
						is_primary_holder_title = yes
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0			
				NOT = {
					FROM = {
						faction_power = {
							faction = faction_pretender
							power = 1.0
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.001
				has_nickname = nick_the_conqueror
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_weak_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = charitable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = content
			}
		}

		log = "[Root.GetBestName] has caved to the claimant faction demand of [From.GetBestName]."

		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_pretender
					letter_event = { id = 8098 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
					set_character_flag = no_need_to_inform
				}
				letter_event = { id = 8061 }
				diplomatic_immunity = no
				set_character_flag = no_need_to_inform
			}
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { has_character_flag = no_need_to_inform }
				}
				character_event = { id = 8099 }
			}
			any_vassal = {
				clr_character_flag = no_need_to_inform
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_strong_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_pretender
						power = 1.0
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_pretender
						power = 1.5
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_pretender
						power = 2.0
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_pretender
						power = 3.0
					}
				}
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					faction_power = {
						faction = faction_pretender
						power = 4.0
					}
				}
			}
		}

		log = "[Root.GetBestName] has refused the claimant faction demand of [From.GetBestName] -- this should start a civil war."

		FROM = {
			tooltip = { any_faction_backer = { faction = faction_pretender } }
			hidden_tooltip = {
				letter_event = { id = 8111 } #inform
				
				#setup faction leader
				diplomatic_immunity = no
				clr_character_flag = faction_claimant_ultimatum_taken
				if = {
					limit = { supported_claimant = { NOT = { character = PREV } } }
					supported_claimant = {
						opinion = { modifier = opinion_very_grateful who = PREV years = 10 }
						reverse_opinion = { modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant who = PREV years = 20 }
					}
				}
				set_character_flag = original_war_liege
				pf_setup_rebel_effect = yes
				
				#setup faction backers
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_pretender
					diplomatic_immunity = no
					supported_claimant = {
						opinion = { modifier = opinion_very_grateful who = PREV years = 10 }
						reverse_opinion = { modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant who = PREV years = 20 }
					}
					pf_setup_rebel_effect = yes
				}
				
				#call claimant into war, if possible
				if = {
					limit = { supported_claimant = { NOT = { vassal_of = ROOT } } }
					supported_claimant = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.423 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		
		#start the actual war
		set_character_flag = faction_pretender_war
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { supported_claimant = { character = PREV } }
				faction_pretender = { # The target (title) of the faction
					reverse_war = {
						target = FROM
						casus_belli = claim_on_liege_plot
						faction = faction_pretender
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { supported_claimant = { character = PREV } }
				}
				faction_pretender = { # The target (title) of the faction
					reverse_war = {
						target = FROM
						casus_belli = other_claim_on_liege_plot
						faction = faction_pretender
					}
				}
			}
		}
	
		#inform remaining vassals
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_vassal = {
				letter_event = { id = PlusFaction.403 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Demand accepted - Install Claimant
letter_event = {
	id = 8061
	desc = "EVTDESC8061"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = faction_claimant_ultimatum_taken
		clr_character_flag = civil_war_faction_leader
		clr_character_flag = civil_war_faction_member
		clr_character_flag = will_join_civil_war
		supported_claimant = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_very_grateful
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant
				who = ROOT
				years = 20
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EXCELLENT"
		supported_claimant = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					prisoner = yes
					host = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							is_liege_or_above = FROM
						}
					}
				}
				prisoner = no
			}
			ROOT = {
				supported_claimant_title = {
					# If the claimant has the wrong government type, take care of that first.
					if = {
						limit = {
							higher_tier_than = PREVPREV
							holder_scope = {
								OR = {
									is_feudal = yes
									is_tribal = yes
									is_nomadic = yes
								}
							}
							ROOT = {
								supported_claimant = {
									is_ruler = yes
									OR = {
										is_theocracy = yes
										is_republic = yes
									}
								}
							}
						}
						ROOT = { 
							supported_claimant = {
								abdicate = { move = no }
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_primary_holder_title = yes
						}
						FROM = {
							any_demesne_title = {
								limit =	{
									is_primary_holder_title_tier = yes
									OR = {
										tier = KING
										tier = EMPEROR
									}
								}
								if = {
									limit = { has_law = crown_authority_1 }
									add_law_w_cooldown = crown_authority_0
								}
								if = {
									limit = { has_law = crown_authority_2 }
									add_law_w_cooldown = crown_authority_1
								}
								if = {
									limit = { has_law = crown_authority_3 }
									add_law_w_cooldown = crown_authority_2
								}
								if = {
									limit = { has_law = crown_authority_4 }
									add_law_w_cooldown = crown_authority_3
								}									
							}
							any_demesne_title = {
								limit = {
									OR = {
										has_law = tribal_organization_1
										has_law = tribal_organization_2
										has_law = tribal_organization_3
										has_law = tribal_organization_4
									}
								}
								if = {
									limit = { has_law = tribal_organization_1 }
									add_law = tribal_organization_0
								}
								if = {
									limit = { has_law = tribal_organization_2 }
									add_law = tribal_organization_1
								}
								if = {
									limit = { has_law = tribal_organization_3 }
									add_law = tribal_organization_2
								}
								if = {
									limit = { has_law = tribal_organization_4 }
									add_law = tribal_organization_3
								}
							}
							any_demesne_title = {
								limit = {
									is_primary_holder_title_tier = yes
									is_primary_holder_title = no
								}
								usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = { target = PREVPREVPREVPREV type = faction_demand }
							}
							primary_title = {
								usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = { target = PREVPREVPREVPREV type = faction_demand }
								hidden_tooltip = { make_primary_title = yes }
							}
							set_defacto_liege = PREVPREVPREV
							pf_liege_change_effect = yes
						}
						hidden_tooltip = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									FROM = {
										ROOT = {
											supported_claimant = {
												primary_title = { 
													NOT = { has_law = succ_feudal_elective } 
													FROM = {
														capital_scope = {
															de_jure_liege_or_above = PREVPREV
														}
													}
												}
											}
										}
										OR = {
											num_of_count_titles = 2
											primary_title = { higher_tier_than = COUNT }
										}
									}
								}
								ROOT = {
									supported_claimant = {
										FROM = {
											capital_scope = {
												county = {
													usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = { target = PREVPREVPREV type = faction_demand }
												}
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}	
						}
						hidden_tooltip = {
							FROM = { 
								set_defacto_liege = PREVPREVPREV
								pf_liege_change_effect = yes								
								any_vassal = {
									limit = {
										NOT = { primary_title = { de_jure_liege_or_above = PREVPREV } }
									}
									set_defacto_liege = PREVPREVPREVPREV
									pf_liege_change_effect = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_primary_holder_title = no
							OR = {
								tier = KING
								tier = EMPEROR
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_law = crown_authority_1 }
							add_law_w_cooldown = crown_authority_0
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_law = crown_authority_2 }
							add_law_w_cooldown = crown_authority_1
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_law = crown_authority_3 }
							add_law_w_cooldown = crown_authority_2
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_law = crown_authority_4 }
							add_law_w_cooldown = crown_authority_3
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_primary_holder_title = no
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_law = tribal_organization_1 }
							add_law = tribal_organization_0
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_law = tribal_organization_2 }
							add_law = tribal_organization_1
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_law = tribal_organization_3 }
							add_law = tribal_organization_2
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_law = tribal_organization_4 }
							add_law = tribal_organization_3
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_primary_holder_title = no
						}
						usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded_and_vassals_no_adj = { target = PREVPREV type = faction_demand }					
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Poisoned Wine - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 8155
	desc = EVTDESC8155
	picture = GFX_evt_feast
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		prisoner = no
		
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8155" # Drinks the wine
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = temperate
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = gluttonous
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = temperate }
						NOT = { trait = gluttonous }
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8163 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8156 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8164 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8157 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8155" # Discovers the poison
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = temperate
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = gluttonous
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = temperate }
					NOT = { trait = gluttonous }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8165 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8158 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8166 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8159 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Falling Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 8175
	desc = "EVTDESC8175"
	picture = GFX_evt_feast
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		prisoner = no
		
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8175" # Falls
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8183 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8176 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8184 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8177 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8175" # Dodges
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8185 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8178 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8186 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8179 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 8179
	desc = "EVTDESC8179"
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8179"
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = paranoid }
				NOT = { trait = trusting }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = paranoid
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = trusting
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				remove_trait = trusting
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
}

	}	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7700" # Hire archers
		trigger = {
			NOT = { martial = 10 }
			NOT = {
				event_target:plot_leader = {
					plot_power = 1.0
				}
			}
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			character_event = { id = 7710 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8160" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7700" # Knows good archers

		trigger = {

			event_target:plot_leader = {
				plot_power = 0.5

		}

			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}

# Archer Ambush - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7705
	desc = "EVTDESC7705"
	picture = GFX_evt_longbowman
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7705" # Hit by arrows
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = craven
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = craven }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7713 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7706 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7714 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7707 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7705" # Avoids arrows
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = craven
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = craven }
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7715 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7708 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7716 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7709 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Manure Explosion - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7725
	desc = "EVTDESC7725"
	picture = GFX_evt_council
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7725" # Blown up
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = diligent
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = diligent }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7733 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7726 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7734 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7727 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7725" # Not blown up
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = diligent
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = diligent }
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7735 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7728 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7736 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7729 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Infanticide - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7745
	desc = "EVTDESC7745"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7745" # Smothered
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = brave
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = gregarious
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = brave }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						NOT = { trait = gregarious }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7753 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7746 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7754 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7747 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7745" # Not smothered
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = brave
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = gregarious
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = gregarious }
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					NOT = { trait = brave }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7755 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7748 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7756 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7749 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		clear_event_target = target_victim
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		tooltip = { dishonorable_plus_1_effect = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = honest
			}
			remove_trait = honest
			
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = kind
			}
			remove_trait = kind
		}
	}
}

# Prison Break - Plot backer requests funds
character_event = {
	id = 7762
	desc = "EVTDESC7762"

	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

		plot_target_char = { save_event_target_as = plot_target }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7762"
		transfer_scaled_wealth = {
				from = ROOT
				to = FROM
				value = 1.0
		}
		FROM = { character_event = { id = 7763 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8153" } }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			event_target:plot_target = { character_event = { id = 7765 days = 27 } }
		}
	}

# Prison Break - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7765
	desc = "EVTDESC7765"
	picture = GFX_evt_into_the_dungeon
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7765" # Tries to escape
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = craven
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = craven }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7773 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7766 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7774 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7767 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7765" # Does not try to escape
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = craven
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = craven }
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7775 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7768 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7776 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7769 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Bathtub Drowning - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7785
	desc = "EVTDESC7785"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7785" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_strong_trigger = yes
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = diligent
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						is_weak_trigger = yes
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = diligent }
						NOT = { is_weak_trigger = yes }
						NOT = { is_strong_trigger = yes }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7793 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7786 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7794 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7787 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7785" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_strong_trigger = yes
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = diligent
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					is_weak_trigger = yes
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = diligent }
					NOT = { is_weak_trigger = yes }
					NOT = { is_strong_trigger = yes }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7795 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7788 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7796 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7789 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Boating Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7805
	desc = "EVTDESC7805"
	picture = GFX_evt_kraken
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7805" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = diligent
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = diligent }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7813 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7806 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7814 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7807 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7805" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_strong_trigger = yes
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = diligent
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					is_weak_trigger = yes
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = diligent }
					NOT = { is_weak_trigger = yes }
					NOT = { is_strong_trigger = yes }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7815 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7808 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7816 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7809 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### POISONOUS SNAKE
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Poisonous Snake
character_event = {
	id = 7820
	desc = "EVTDESC7820"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			has_plot = plot_take_revenge
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			NOT = { is_murder_quest_target_of_prev_trigger = yes }
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			prisoner = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 500
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75

	id = 7822
	desc = "EVTDESC7822"
	picture = GFX_evt_spymaster
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		plot_target_char = { save_event_target_as = plot_target }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7822"
		transfer_scaled_wealth = {
				from = ROOT
				to = FROM
				value = 1.0
		}
		FROM = { character_event = { id = 7823 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8153" } }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			event_target:plot_target = { character_event = { id = 7825 days = 27 } }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8152"
		FROM = { character_event = { id = 7824 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8154" } }
	}
}

# Poisonous Snake - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7825
	desc = "EVTDESC7825"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7825" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = craven
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = slothful
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = craven }
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						NOT = { trait = slothful }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7833 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7826 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7834 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7827 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7825" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = craven
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = slothful
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = craven }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					NOT = { trait = slothful }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7835 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7828 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7836 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7829 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 7840
	desc = "EVTDESC7840"

	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			has_plot = plot_take_revenge
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			NOT = { is_murder_quest_target_of_prev_trigger = yes }
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			prisoner = no

		}

						power = 0.90
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					has_plot = plot_take_revenge
				}
				plot_power = 0.5
				plot_target_char = {
					NOT = { is_murder_quest_target_of_prev_trigger = yes }
					is_adult = yes
					NOT = { trait = incapable }
					NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
					prisoner = no
				}
				NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
				ROOT = {
					plot_power_contribution = 
					{
						plotter = PREV
						power = 0.025
					}
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = plot_leader
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7840" # The conspirators bribe servants
		trigger = {
			event_target:plot_leader = {
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			character_event = { id = 7850 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8160" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8151" # Ask the Plotter for funds
		trigger = {
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
			NOT = {
				event_target:plot_leader = {
					plot_power = 1.0
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:plot_leader = {
			character_event = { id = 7842 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8152" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7840" # Bribe servants

			NOT = {

					plot_power = 1.0
				}

# Balcony Plummet - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7845
	desc = "EVTDESC7845"
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7845" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = diligent
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						NOT = { trait = diligent }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7853 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7846 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7854 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7847 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7845" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = diligent
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = diligent }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7855 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7848 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7856 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7849 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Hunting Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7865
	desc = "EVTDESC7865"
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7865" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = gregarious
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						NOT = { trait = gregarious }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7873 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7866 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7874 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7867 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7865" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = gregarious
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					NOT = { trait = gregarious }
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7875 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7868 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7876 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7869 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

		}
	}

# Disguised Highwaymen - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7885
	desc = "EVTDESC7885"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7885" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = diligent
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						NOT = { trait = diligent }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7893 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7886 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7894 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7887 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7885" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = diligent
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = diligent }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7895 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7888 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7896 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7889 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Disguised Highwaymen - Notification: Success, but discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7893
	desc = "EVTDESC7893"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		character_event = { id = 10 } # Consequences of discovery
		clear_event_target = target_victim
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8163"
		tooltip = { dishonorable_plus_1_effect = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = honest
			}
			remove_trait = honest
			
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = kind
			}
			remove_trait = kind
		}
	}
}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Carriage Accident
character_event = {
	id = 7900
	desc = "EVTDESC7900"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			has_plot = plot_take_revenge
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			NOT = { is_murder_quest_target_of_prev_trigger = yes }
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			prisoner = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 500
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_character_modifier = plot_assisted_spying
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.60
			has_character_modifier = plot_assisted_spying2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.45
			has_character_modifier = plot_assisted_spying3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.30
			has_character_modifier = plot_assisted_spying4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.15
			has_character_modifier = plot_assisted_spying5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			plot_target_char = { check_variable = { which = "personal_spy_network" value = 10 } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			plot_target_char = { check_variable = { which = "personal_spy_network" value = 20 } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			plot_target_char = { check_variable = { which = "personal_spy_network" value = 30 } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			plot_target_char = { check_variable = { which = "personal_spy_network" value = 40 } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			plot_target_char = { check_variable = { which = "personal_spy_network" value = 50 } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power = 1.5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power = 2.0
		}

			factor = 0.66
			plot_power = 3.0

			factor = 0.66
			plot_power = 4.0
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power = 6.0
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power = 8.0
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			plot_power = 10.0
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			plot_power_contribution =
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			plot_power_contribution =
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			plot_power_contribution =
			{

			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			plot_power_contribution =
			{
				plotter = ROOT

			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			plot_power_contribution =
			{
				plotter = ROOT

			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			plot_power_contribution =
			{
				plotter = ROOT

			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			plot_power_contribution =
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			plot_power_contribution =
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			plot_power_contribution =
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			plot_power_contribution =
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		plot_target_char = { save_event_target_as = plot_target }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7900" # The conspirators bribe the servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				character_event = { id = 7912 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		event_target:plot_target = { character_event = { id = 7905 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7905" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7900" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -1.0
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				character_event = { id = 7912 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		event_target:plot_target = { character_event = { id = 7905 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7905" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7900" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				character_event = { id = 7912 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		event_target:plot_target = { character_event = { id = 7905 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7905" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7900" # Replace with own servants
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			intrigue = 10
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				character_event = { id = 7912 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		event_target:plot_target = { character_event = { id = 7905 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7905" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}
}

# Carriage Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7905
	desc = "EVTDESC7905"
	picture = GFX_evt_carriage
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7905" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = diligent
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = diligent }
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7913 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7906 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7914 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7907 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7905" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = diligent
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = diligent }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7915 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7908 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7916 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7909 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Decadent Debauchery - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7955
	desc = "EVTDESC7955"
	picture = GFX_evt_jugglers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				has_plot = plot_take_revenge
			}
			plot_target_char = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7955" # Dies
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = slothful
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = proud
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = hedonist
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = gluttonous
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = drunkard
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					trait = lustful
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = drunkard }
					NOT = { trait = hedonist }
					NOT = { trait = lustful }
					NOT = { trait = gluttonous }
					NOT = { trait = slothful }
					NOT = { trait = proud }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7963 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7956 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7964 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7957 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7955" # Does not die
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = slothful
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = proud
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = hedonist
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = gluttonous
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = drunkard
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						trait = lustful
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = drunkard }
						NOT = { trait = hedonist }
						NOT = { trait = lustful }
						NOT = { trait = gluttonous }
						NOT = { trait = slothful }
						NOT = { trait = proud }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7965 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7958 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7966 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7959 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = 7500
	desc = "EVTDESC7500"

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_liege_of = FROM
		FROM = { has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal }
	}
	
	option = { #Yes
		name = "EVTOPTA7500"
		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 7501 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7501" }
			plot_target_char = {
				letter_event = { id = 7504 days = 4 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7504A" }
			}
		}
 		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					trait = just
					NOT = {
						opinion = { who = FROM value = -10 }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				trait = deceitful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					plot_target_char = {
						ROOT = {
							likes_better_than = { who = PREV than = FROM }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #No
		name = "EVTOPTB7500"
		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 7502 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7502" }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					plot_target_char = {
						ROOT = {
							likes_better_than = { who = FROM than = PREV }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

letter_event = {
	id = 8200
	desc = EVTDESC8200
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {

	}
	
	immediate = {

				faction = faction_antiking
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8000
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					FROM = {
						faction_power =

							faction = faction_antiking
							power = 1.0
						}
					}
				}
			}

			}

				factor = 1.25

			}

				factor = 1.25
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {

				trait = charitable
			}

				factor = 1.25
				trait = patient
			}

				factor = 1.25
				trait = content
			}
		}

			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { in_faction = faction_antiking }
				}
				character_event = { id = 8202 }
			}

				letter_event = { id = 8203 }
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_antiking
					letter_event = { id = 8201 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			religion_authority = {
				modifier = deposed_antipope
				years = 50
			}
			faction_antiking = { # The target (title) of the faction
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = investiture_law_1 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = investiture_law_0
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						religion = catholic
					}
					k_papal_state = {
						holder_scope = {
							opinion = {
								who = PREVPREV
								modifier = opinion_deposed_antipope
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						religion = fraticelli
					}

						holder_scope = {
							opinion = {
								who = PREVPREV
								modifier = opinion_deposed_antipope
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			rightful_religious_head_scope = {
				remove_claim = k_papal_state
				remove_claim = d_fraticelli
			}
		}
		
		primary_title = {
			usurp_title = FROM
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_strong_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				FROM = {
					faction_power = 
					{
						faction = faction_antiking
						power = 1.5
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					faction_power = 
					{
						faction = faction_antiking
						power = 1.0
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					faction_power = 
					{

						power = 2.0
					}

						power = 3.0
					}
				}

				}

				}

				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {

			tooltip = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_antiking
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {

					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
						}
						30 = {

						}

							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {

					}

						}

						}

				if = {
					limit = { has_law = law_voting_power_0 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = law_voting_power_1
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = war_voting_power_0 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = war_voting_power_1
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = revoke_title_voting_power_0 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = revoke_title_voting_power_1
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = imprison_voting_power_0 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = imprison_voting_power_1
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = grant_title_voting_power_0 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = grant_title_voting_power_1
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = banish_voting_power_0 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = banish_voting_power_1
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = execution_voting_power_0 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = execution_voting_power_1
					break = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 8
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				is_strong_trigger = yes
			}

				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {

				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = stubborn
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					faction_power = 
					{
						faction = faction_increase_council_power
						power = 1.5
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					faction_power = 
					{
						faction = faction_increase_council_power
						power = 1.0
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {

				FROM = {
					faction_power =

letter_event = {
	id = 8221
	desc = "EVTDESC8221"
	
	show_from_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "GOOD"
		reverse_opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_grateful
			who = FROMFROM
			years = 5
		}

		if = {
			limit = { event_target:new_title_holder = { NOT = { character = ROOT } } }
			add_favor = event_target:new_title_holder
			opinion = {
				who = event_target:new_title_holder
				modifier = opinion_favorite
				years = 5
			}
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = faction_powerful_vassal_takeover_ultimatum_timer
			hidden = yes
			duration = 3650
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 8226
	desc = "EVTDESC8226"
	picture = GFX_evt_coronation
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		primary_title = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT =  { has_law = succ_feudal_elective } }
				add_law_w_cooldown = succ_feudal_elective
			}
		}

	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8226"
		clr_character_flag = new_title_holder
		job_chancellor = { remove_title = job_chancellor }
		job_marshal = { remove_title = job_marshal }
		job_treasurer = { remove_title = job_treasurer }
		job_spymaster = { remove_title = job_spymaster }
		job_spiritual = { remove_title = job_spiritual }
		any_vassal = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = helped_win_war
			}
			character_event = { id = 8225 days = 1 }
			tooltip = {
				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_favorite
					years = 5
				}
				reverse_add_favor = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}
